Four turns needed! ! While improving the privacy of staying guests, the check-in route is slightly tortuous. However, the smiles greeting you all the way and the wonderful art displays and installations around the corner make the twists and turns of arrival a little necessary.
hotel room:
There are two types: light wood grain with Prada green marble and dark wood grain with violet marble. Because I had children, I chose the dark wood grain vision twin room on the higher floor. The dark wood grain texture is very good. The same golden arch element at the entrance is matched with the bright checkered wooden floor. In addition, the top surface requires high craftsmanship and beveled side roof. Finally, like the Guangzhou Four Seasons, the bathroom has walls and floors covered with violet marble, continuing Showing you luxury and elegance all the way.
Key points: 2 twin rooms with a width of 1.5 meters. Guests traveling with children may find it great.
Public area floor:
4F is the spa fitness area with Internet celebrity time corridor.
From the elevator to the reception hall, the unique smell and the gentle sound of running water make your five senses immediately feel tranquil and relaxed. Each aisle is carefully designed and you feel as if you have passed through a maze and across time and space.
The dazzling details of the coffee shop on the 5th floor, which is surrounded by flowers and green plants with a malachite green theme, may look a bit messy from the photos, but in person they feel that they complement each other. It is recommended that if you stay, you must stay here for an afternoon and have a red velvet cake. If the weather is not so hot, it would be better to feel the breeze outside by the French garden.
The 6th floor, connected to the 5th floor through a white marble spiral staircase, is the magnificent breakfast room - Huiyi Western Restaurant. When you look up at the metal embossed ceiling, you may be as surprised as me. Only the seats in the booths are too shallow, making it difficult to feel comfortable. It is worth mentioning that the whiskey bar hidden in the connecting part on the 4th and 5th floors is the best Easter egg of this stay. The bar manager is a top archeology student who can recite the Romance of the Three Kingdoms. Three snacks, three glasses of whiskey, from the second use of oak barrels, to the different aroma cups, to the 57.1-proof domestic whiskey, I sat here almost all night.

The porter will also actively help to open the door and take the luggage.
If you like to enjoy the facilities and services of an old five-star hotel, Waldorf Astoria is no problem, but at this price in Xiamen, Qishang and Conrad are more cost-effective.

The design concept of Waldorf Astoria Xiamen is "elegant manor", the whole hotel has both Nanyang style and European luxury style. A large number of curved designs are used in the hotel, which is very high-end; the use of green plants and floral art makes the hotel full of vitality.

I personally like the color of the hotel room very much. There are two color systems. The dark wood room is equipped with a brown marble bathroom, which is stable and elegant, and the light wood room is equipped with a green marble bathroom, which has a stylish and bright feeling. It is said that these two different color systems, the dark color is inspired by the orange brown tea color, paying tribute to the tea culture of Xiamen; the water green is inspired by the tranquil a**osphere of the seaside.

What's amazing is the hotel's constant temperature outdoor sun swimming pool, which is disinfected with sea salt, which does not smell like the usual swimming pool disinfection water. The terrace garden next to the swimming pool is lush with greenery, which really makes people feel like being in an elegant manor.
